  <h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0642857s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><strong> </strong></h1>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1629948816092_3005"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628654845578_5821"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div></div><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-4 span-4"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html sqs-background-enabled preSlide slideIn" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:30.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:30.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:30.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:30.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1629948816092_3072" data-classes="" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0669643s;"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0696429s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em>Our Learning Approach</em></span></h3><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0723214s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong><em>Play-based learning</em></strong></span><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em> is an effective learning approach in our curriculum, especially for our young learners in Nursery classes, given their innate curiosity and ability to learn effectively through exploration, self-discovery, experimentation and imagination.  We engage  our children in both indoor and outdoor play for effective and fun hands-on learning  through concrete experiences, play and field trips. Interactive thematic learning corners are designed to facilitate active learning through play.</em></span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.075s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em>At the Kindergartener levels, our active learners participate in</em></span><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><em> </em><strong><em>inquiry-based learning</em></strong></span><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em> and </em></span><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong><em>guided project work</em></strong></span><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em> integrated across multiple learning domains. They will answer open-ended and thought-provoking questions and participate in the process of inquiry, where they investigate, explore and formulate creative solutions to build their foundation for higher-order thinking skills. They will present their works to their peers and teachers to develop their confidence and communication skills.</em></span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0776786s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><em>Our guiding principle is always to make childrens learning effective and enjoyable so that they learn joyfully and confidently, gaining a head start in school readiness and lifelong learning. We are passionate in enabling every child to reach his/ her potential and to be future-ready, with the mindsets of an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur.</em></span></p>
</div>

    <div class="content">
      
      
      
      
      
      
      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-620ccc0f01b27a255955ac0b"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-dafd2bac1a4ecfa00fcb"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0803571s;" class="preSlide slideIn">Distinctive Methodist Preschool Curriculum </h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0830357s;">Our group of Methodist preschools offer an integrated thematic <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Core-Curriculum-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent"><strong>Core Curriculum</strong></span></a> with comprehensive coverage of the six learning domains for holistic development in accordance with MOEs Nurturing Early Learners (NEL) curriculum. It is designed based on established <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Educational_Strategies"><strong>Education Strategies</strong></a> and encompasses both academic and character development.</p><p class="sqsrte-small preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0857143s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0883929s;">To extend the holistic learning and development of our young minds beyond the core curriculum, centres offering 4-hour programmes also offer an <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Extended-Curriculum-section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent"><strong>Extended Curriculum</strong></span></a> that features various STEM-based <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Applied-Learning-Programme-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black"><strong><em>Applied Learning Programme</em></strong></span></a><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black"> modules. The </span>wide spread of hands-on learning activities and experiences develops multiple areas of intelligence to develop future-ready attributes of explorers, innovators and entrepreneurs in our young minds. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0910714s;">All our centres also offer the enriching <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Explorers-Programme-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black"><strong><em>Explorers Programme</em></strong></span></a><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black"><strong><em> </em></strong></span>that develops practical life-skills and soft skills as well as character development based on biblical values.</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.09375s;">At Methodist Preschool, our team of highly qualified curriculum specialists regularly review, update and enhance our programmes to meet the evolving learning needs of our children, in teaching and nurturing the next generation of contributing and responsible citizens. In support of our commitment to nurture every child to be a person of Good Character with future-ready attributes of an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur, we offer 3 distinctive <a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Signature-Programmes-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent"><strong>Signature Programmes</strong></span></a> :</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0964286s;"><strong><em>Signature K2 Space Buds Programme</em></strong></p></li><li><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0991071s;"><strong><em>Proprietary Music Programme</em></strong></p></li><li><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.101786s;"><strong><em>Applied Learning Programme</em></strong><em> (part of our Extended Curriculum)</em></p></li></ul><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.104464s;"></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.107143s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">To harness the benefits of education technology to in enhancing both our teaching and learning processes, </span><a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Innovative-Education-Technology-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent"><strong>Innovative Education Technology</strong></span></a><a href="https://methodistpreschools.org/our-approach-curriculum/#Innovative-Technology-Section"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent"><strong> </strong></span></a><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black"> is integrated in the delivery of some curriculum components within our core and extended programmes. </span>The use of carefully-selected coding and reading robots effectively stimulates, engages and challenges our preschoolers to maximise the effectiveness and fun of learning. </p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block button-block sqs-block-button" data-block-type="53" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1645008549388_24517"><div class="sqs-block-content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_608">

  <h3 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.1125s;" class="preSlide"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent">Distinctive Methodist Preschool Education</span></h3>
</div>

  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.117857s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent">Our Signature Programmes</span></h2>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1645049280810_28195"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="spacebuds-section" class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.120536s;">
  </p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1664357611241_27552"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.123214s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>Signature K2 Space Buds Programme</strong></span></h3><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.125893s;">Our Space Buds is a one-of-a-kind education programme designed to introduce our K2 children to all things Space and excite them about the final frontier through a purposeful and intentional approach. It is designed to fire up the young sparks to build lifelong interest and foundational knowledge in Space and STEM at an early age. We bring purposeful fun and passion together to create an environment that educates, spurs creativity, and ignites their passion for learning and appreciation for innovation.</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.128571s;">The Space Buds Programme is conducted in two phases for our K2 cohort. Phase One comprises Space lessons taught by industry experts from Space Faculty (an organization with the mission to create the next generation of global tech leaders starting with Space) in April, in conjunction with the United Nations (U.N.). International Day of Human Space Flight on 12 April annually. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.13125s;">Phase Two of the Space Buds Programme is conducted in early October, when our family of Methodist preschools joins the world in celebrating World Space Week (4-10 Oct) - an international celebration of the contribution of space science and technology to the betterment of the human condition. Our preschools engage children with a kaleidoscope of exciting lessons and activities designed to spark our little explorers' curiosity, imagination, interest, exploration and learning of Space. From our youngest child in Nursery to our K2 children, the myriad of hands-on and fun activities that are specially curated and prepared to engage our young minds promise to be a blast! The highlight of World Space Week for our graduating batch of K2 students will be the exclusive opportunity for them to participate in a live virtual interactive learning session with a NASA Astronaut to hear the first-hand sharing of their experience as an Astronaut. Best of all, our young minds' burning questions get answered during the interactive Q&amp;A session during the virtual meet-up.</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.133929s;">The <strong>Signature Space Buds Programme</strong> is a definite highlight for every Methodist preschooler before they graduate. We are confident the unique learning experience will go a long way to fueling children's passion and curiosity as lifelong learners and helping them become future-ready.</p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1645163306050_24450"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1645163306050_28236"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.136607s;" class="preFade fadeIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--custom" style="color: #FF0438"><strong>Methodist Preschool Space Learning Programme</strong></span></h4>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_434"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_433"><div class="sqs-block image-block sqs-block-image sqs-text-ready" data-block-type="5" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1682901512002_17748"><div class="sqs-block-content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_432">

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-620cd1c27f29ad1851c2698a"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_491"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_490"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-8e39ce25812ee4e6b145"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.184821s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>Signature Methodist Music Odyssey Programme</strong></span></h3><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.1875s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white"><strong>The Methodist Music Odyssey programme</strong> is a signature programme developed with the Methodist School of Music and taught in Methodist preschools to provide every child with access to high-quality music experiences in their preschool education.</span></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.190179s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white">Research has shown that exposure to music from early childhood onwards helps children speak more clearly, develop a more extensive vocabulary, and strengthen social and emotional skills. Music education has proven benefits of accelerating the development of language and numeracy skills, enhancing memory, inspiring creativity and building self-confidence. It can also energize, build rapport, set the tone for the day, stimulate the mind and facilitate fun and inspiration. </span></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.192857s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--white">Children will start their early music journey learning to enjoy and appreciate music through music &amp; movement, singing and music making. At K1 and K2 levels, the programme aims to develop the whole child with a musical and spiritual emphasis. The rich and unique music curriculum engages the whole Methodist approach to lay the foundation for godly character through holistic music education. </span></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.195536s;"></p><p style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.198214s;" class="preFade fadeIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong><em>The MMO programme adopts the principles of the Kodly concept of holistic music education across six domains:</em></strong></span></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.211607s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--darkAccent">Our Extended Curriculum </span></h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.214286s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">Children enrolled in our Extended Curriculum programme enjoy a rich palette of hands-on learning activities and experiences that stretches their holistic development in multiple areas.  Our Extended Curriculum** comprises a spread of STEM-based modules under the <strong>Applied Learning Programme.</strong></span></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.216964s;"></p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.222321s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent">Applied Learning Programme </span></h3><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.225s;">Our enriching Applied Learning Programme (ALP) aims to foster creative and critical thinking and practise the skills necessary to excel in project-based environments through the application of S.T.E.M (Science, Technology, Engineering and Mathematics) education.  The wide range of modules conducted during different terms of the year seek to inspire exploration, innovation and develop attributes of entrepreneurship to future-proof our preschoolers :</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap;                       <h2 class="list-item-content__title preSlide slideIn" style="max-width: 100%; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.2625s;">LEGO Build the Change</h2>
                    

                    
                        <div class="list-item-content__description
                          
                          " style="
                            margin-top: 4%;
                            max-width: 100%;
                          "><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.265179s;">Methodist Preschool collaborates with LEGO Group to run the Build The Change programme to educate our preschoolers about global warming and the importance of environmental protection. Our little innovators are challenged to exercise their creativity using LEGO bricks to build imaginative solutions to address the adverse effects of climate change. The programmes climax is most certainly the opportunity for students to present their creative builds during a show-and-tell session to peers and teachers. Its never too young to be a Builder of Change!</p></div>

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-632c132214416c2c21aaf1a0"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1663832958861_24073"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="Explorers-Programme-Section" class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.35625s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-3d24e659af40a3c30720"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.358929s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent">Explorers Programme</span></h3><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.361607s;">The BB Explorers Programme is an integrated preschool values-in-action community development programme by the Boys and Girls Brigade Singapore. It develops practical life-skills and soft skills as well as character development based on biblical values. Through life lessons or stories, hands-on activities and fun games, children learn essential life skills while building important character values and attributes. Motor skills, social skills and creativity are enhanced through the engaging activities too. The little explorers embark on a 4 Dimensional Journey through 4 Discovery Islands with the objectives of discovering the world around them, their place in the world, the needs of others and to discover themselves through the comprehensive Explorers Programme.</p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>
  
</section>

    <div class="content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_508">
      
      
      
      
      
      
      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-620ccbb23e1ddb4ba9ae958a"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_507"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_506"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1663831250190_45287"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="Innovative-Education-Technology-section" class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.39375s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-6517679a7e5189b4664a"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.396429s;" class="preSlide slideIn">Innovative Education Technology</h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.399107s;">Creative integration of innovative education technology within our curriculum enhances both teaching and learning processes. The use of smart interactive technology effectively stimulates, engages and challenges our preschoolers to maximise the effectiveness and fun of learning. Our students digital competence is also developed in the process as we future-proof them to learn, work and live in an increasingly technology-dependent society into the 21st century. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.401786s;">The Luka AI Reading Robot, Bee Bot and Tale-Bot Coding Robots are among the first initiatives in educational technology that have been rolled out at some of our Methodist preschools, with more in store in line with our curriculum advancement to orientate our students toward future readiness in our Smart Nation and a highly digitalised world that they are part of.</p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_505"><div class="col sqs-col-7 span-7"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer" data-aspect-ratio="9.476309226932669" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1669615461036_20523" data-classes=""><div class="sqs-block-content sqs-intrinsic" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_654" style="padding-bottom: 9.47631%;">&nbsp;</div></div><div class="sqs-block video-block sqs-block-video" data-block-json="{&quot;blockAnimation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;,&quot;layout&quot;:&quot;caption-hidden&quot;,&quot;overlay&quot;:false,&quot;description&quot;:{},&quot;hSize&quot;:null,&quot;floatDir&quot;:null,&quot;isOldBlock&quot;:false,&quot;html&quot;:&quot;<iframe class=\&quot;embedly-embed\&quot; <div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p style="text-align: right; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.404464s;" class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong><em>Methodist Preschool is a proud Winner of the Gartner 2022 Eye on Innovation Awards in Education for the use of the LUKA AI Reading Robot to enhance Chinese language learning in our curriculum. The award recognises education institutions for their innovative use of technology to drive best-in-class initiatives.</em></strong></span></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-5 span-5" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_504"><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-838744bdc38317225a74"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1669618478518_22463"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="LUKA" class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.407143s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-c8d1cb4b44e0d1408356"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.409821s;" class="preFade fadeIn">Luka AI Reading Robot</h4><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.4125s;"><em>First of its kind to debut in a preschool in Singapore, Luka is an interactive reading robot built with cutting-edge AI technology. </em>It reads aloud bilingual picture books placed in front of him, page by page. In addition to over 20,000 English picture books and 70,000 Chinese titles stored in its sizeable cloud storage, Luka has the capability of voice recording, hence read-along sessions featuring a personalised voice can be customized. Luka can even play music and sing nursery rhymes for children!</p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.417857s;" class="preFade">Bee Bot Coding Robot</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.420536s;">Bee Bots are used in the teaching of multiple subjects, from languages to Math and Science in both our Core and Extended Curriculums in some of our Methodist preschools. Learning to programme these cute, smiley, wide-eyed educational bee robots sharpen our preschoolers logical thinking and improve our preschoolers' spatial visualisation skills while having fun. It develops their sequential thinking while encouraging creative problem-solving skills when engaging assigned tasks. Children also learn to reflect and persevere when faced with challenges which are essential mindsets for future-readiness!</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.423214s;"></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.428571s;" class="preFade"></h4><h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.43125s;" class="preFade">Tale-Bot Coding Robot</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.433929s;">Tale-Bot is a learning robot specially designed preschoolers with intelligent interactive technology and voice command functions help develop storytelling and computational thinking skills. Its appealing design and features draw children to interact and learn with it. Tale-Bot has livened up the spectrum of Chinese lessons and activities conducted during our Extended Curriculum. </p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.444643s;" class="preSlide">&nbsp;Our Core Curriculum</h2><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.447321s;">Our Methodist preschools offer a uniquely curated curriculum that extends beyond the key learning areas and learning goals stipulated within the Ministry of Educations Nurturing Early Learners (NEL) Curriculum Framework: </p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.45s;">Values, Social and Emotional Development and Learning Dispositions</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.452679s;">Aesthetics and Creative Expression</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.455357s;">Discovery of the World</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.458036s;">Language and Literacy</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.460714s;">Health, Safety and Motor Skills Development</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.463393s;">Numeracy </p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.466071s;">We ensure a comprehensive curriculum that supports the holistic development of children during their early learning and development that aligns with the NEL Framework on the beliefs and teaching principles on how children learn and develop and what constitutes quality preschool education to prepare children to maximize their potential for a bright future ahead. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.46875s;">We adopt a <strong>STEM-based</strong> curriculum. STEM is an acronym for Science, Technology,  Engineering and Mathematics, is an educational discipline that aims to spark an interest and lifelong love of sciences for students to develop a strong foundation on the competencies needed to prepare them for future-readiness. </p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>

</span></a></li><li><a class="c-tabs__tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" id="tab-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" href="#tabpanel-aesthetics-and-creative-expression"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title">Aesthetics and Creative Expression</span></a></li><li><a class="c-tabs__tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel-discovery-of-the-world-" id="tab-discovery-of-the-world-" href="#tabpanel-discovery-of-the-world-"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title">Discovery of the World

</span></a></li></ul><div class="c-tabs__content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2379"><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="tabpanel-values,-social-and-emotional-development-and-learning-dispositions-" id="tab-values,-social-and-emotional-development-and-learning-dispositions-" href="#tabpanel-values,-social-and-emotional-development-and-learning-dispositions-" aria-expanded="true" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title">Values, Social and <br data-preserve-html-node="true">Emotional Development and <br data-preserve-html-node="true">Learning Dispositions
</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-values,-social-and-emotional-development-and-learning-dispositions-" id="tabpanel-values,-social-and-emotional-development-and-learning-dispositions-"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2378"><div id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2377"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_961"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628158667516_12311"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.471429s;" class="preFade">Values,  Social and Emotional Development and Learning Dispositions</h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.474107s;"><strong>John Wesley, the founder of Methodism, believes that the heart of education is the education of the heart. </strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.476786s;">At Methodist preschools, we take great responsibility in every child's character development as an integral part of our curriculum. Our unique character development programme focuses on our core values of Love, Respect, Courage, Thankfulness and Passion for Learning. Children participate actively in meaningful values-in-action projects and community-based initiatives that shape their character and instil lifelong values, laying a strong foundation for their future success. </p>
</div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" id="tab-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" href="#tabpanel-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title">Aesthetics and Creative Expression</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" id="tabpanel-aesthetics-and-creative-expression" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2425"><div id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2424"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_1268"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628158667516_24043"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.479464s;" class="preFade">Aesthetics and Creative Expression (Music &amp; Art)</h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.482143s;">Our proprietary music programme, developed by the Methodist School of Music and taught by trained music teachers, is a niche in our curriculum. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.484821s;">The rich music appreciation curriculum engages children in learning singing, music and movement and music-making. Our teachers use various techniques to engage children with fun music activities to learn about elements of music, playing instruments, circle games, creative movements, dancing and listening to music. At K1 and K2 levels, the programme aims to develop the whole child with a musical and spiritual emphasis. The rich and unique music curriculum engages the whole Methodist approach to lay the foundation for godly character through holistic music education.  </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.4875s;">Aesthetics involves the creative expression of emotions and ideas. There are many opportunities for children to experiment with colours, lines, shapes, and textures to express themselves creatively and develop a creative imagination and an appreciation of the arts. They will create individual art creations, as well as work in group art projects that promote collaboration and teamwork and, at the same time, stimulate and encourage creativity, exploration and innovation.  </p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_1267"><div class="sqs-block gallery-block sqs-block-gallery" data-block-json="{&quot;hSize&quot;:null,&quot;floatDir&quot;:null,&quot;methodOption&quot;:&quot;transient&quot;,&quot;existingGallery&quot;:null,&quot;newWindow&quot;:false,&quot;transparentBackground&quot;:true,&quot;aspectRatio&quot;:null,&quot;auto-crop&quot;:false,&quot;autoplay&quot;:true,&quot;autoplay-duration&quot;:3,&quot;blockAnimation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;,&quot;collectionId&quot;:&quot;61370977984b3672195c9206&quot;,&quot;controls&quot;:false,&quot;design&quot;:&quot;slideshow&quot;,&quot;show-meta&quot;:false,&quot;show-meta-basic&quot;:true,&quot;show-meta-only-title&quot;:false,&quot;show-meta-only-description&quot;:false,&quot;square-thumbs&quot;:true,&quot;thumbnails&quot;:false,&quot;vSize&quot;:null,&quot;transientGalleryId&quot;:&quot;61370977984b3672195c9206&quot;}" data-block-type="8" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1630996570106_53265"><div class="sqs-block-content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_1266">

</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-discovery-of-the-world-" id="tabpanel-discovery-of-the-world-" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2462"><div id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2461"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_1532"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628154180300_30828"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.490179s;" class="preFade"><strong>Discovery of the World</strong></h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.492857s;">We believe that children are natural explorers, ready to dive headfirst into the wonders of the world. Our passionate teachers are dedicated to fostering their curiosity and empowering them to discover and interact with their surroundings, whether it is their home, school, community, or beyond. Through hands-on experiences and thought-provoking discussions, children will gain a deep understanding of the world around them. Our inquiry-based approach nurtures their logical and thinking skills, encouraging them to ask questions, make observations, and draw meaningful conclusions. From predicting outcomes to conducting investigations  they will learn invaluable process skills that will stay with them for a lifetime.</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.495536s;"></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.498214s;" class="preFade">Language &amp; Literacy</h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.500893s;">Methodist preschools strongly emphasize children's language and literacy development and have carefully crafted a literacy programme for children to soar in! We seamlessly foster listening, speaking, reading, and writing skills through the whole language learning approach. Our passionate educators act as language models, nurturing children's love for language in a supportive and enriching environment.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.503571s;">Phonological awareness supports children in becoming independent, fluent readers. They learn to blend sounds to read new words independently and decode the sounds to spell and write. Stories from various genres, rhymes, songs, language activities and drama are weaved into lessons to make the language meaningful and purposeful. During 'Show &amp; Tell' sessions and class discussions, children confidently speak up and verbalize their feelings, ideas and thoughts. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.50625s;">We understand learning Chinese can be challenging for children! Traditional teaching methods often fail to engage young learners, making the learning process ineffective, and children feel disconnected from grasping and embracing this valuable language. Our curriculum is carefully curated to make learning Chinese fun and engaging. With daily lessons filled with captivating stories, songs, rhymes, creative thematic activities, and a cute-looking AI reading robot, Luka, we create an enjoyable and immersive environment that supports children's language development. Let children experience the joy of learning Chinese with Methodist preschools!</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.508929s;"></p>
</div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--health,-safety-and-motor-skills-development" id="tab--health,-safety-and-motor-skills-development" href="#tabpanel--health,-safety-and-motor-skills-development" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"> Health, Safety and Motor Skills <br data-preserve-html-node="true">Development</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--health,-safety-and-motor-skills-development" id="tabpanel--health,-safety-and-motor-skills-development" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2545"><div id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2544"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2117"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628154180300_33758"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.511607s;" class="preFade">Health, Safety and Motor Skills Development</h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.514286s;">Children are natural movers! Our teachers plan various physical activities to support the development of children's gross locomotor and fine motor skills. They also impact knowledge of good health habits to achieve healthy growth, the importance of safety and how to prevent danger at home, in school and public places, helping children grow in confidence and self-esteem to make safe and healthy choices and lead an active lifestyle in later life. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.516964s;">Every  Methodist preschool features well-equipped facilities, e.g. playground, music room, gym room, cycling arena, sensory water and sand play areas, and resources to support children in developing their motor skills.  </p>
</div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel-numeracy-" id="tab-numeracy-" href="#tabpanel-numeracy-" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title">Numeracy<br data-preserve-html-node="true"> 
</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-numeracy-" id="tabpanel-numeracy-" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2564"><div id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2563"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711764095132_2267"><div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628154180300_35008"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.519643s;" class="preFade">Numeracy</h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.522321s;">At Methodist preschools, our teachers teach numeracy concepts and skills in ways children can understand and apply meaningfully in their daily experiences. The hands-on learning approach effectively supports children in learning numeracy concepts and prepares them for a smooth transition to primary school.   </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.525s;">Children explore and learn numeracy concepts and skills such as relationships and patterns, counting and number sense, shapes and spatial concepts, measurements and visual discrimination, addition and subtraction, time and value of money. Learning corners are thoughtfully designed with concrete objects, resources and activities to facilitate practice and reinforcement of concepts and skills taught. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.527679s;">In centres that adopted the innovative Singapore Preschool Math Curriculum programme, every lesson begins with a story and ends with problem-solving using specially designed manipulatives. </p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.530357s;"></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.546429s;">Children will develop meaningful connections to understand the world they live in. They will share their interests and experiences with their peers and work collaboratively. As they participate in different learning situations, they learn to think, apply, translate and present their creative solutions.</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.549107s;"></p>
</div>

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
